    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app',

<div id="review_2856634049" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2856634049" />
    <a title="AKbar" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/62404396-akbar"><img alt="AKbar" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1481376499p2/62404396.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2856634049?book_show_action=true">Jun 21, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AKbar" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AKbar" href="/user/show/62404396-akbar">AKbar</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2856634049" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3153606710079640000">Economics is not my favorite subject while this book tells about a story of young financial consultant. However, this book offers me an interesting issue related to my country, and so I bought the novel immediately (well actually, this is because I want to escape from news and hoaxes about something happened two months ago in Indonesia). <br/><br/>This is my first read of Tere Liye's book. Reading this novel was like I was standing as among the characters of the novel, witnessing all of the exciting, thri</span>
  <span id="freeText3153606710079640000" style="display:none">Economics is not my favorite subject while this book tells about a story of young financial consultant. However, this book offers me an interesting issue related to my country, and so I bought the novel immediately (well actually, this is because I want to escape from news and hoaxes about something happened two months ago in Indonesia). <br /><br />This is my first read of Tere Liye's book. Reading this novel was like I was standing as among the characters of the novel, witnessing all of the exciting, thrilling adventures of the protagonist, Thomas. For me who are new to reading this type of story, Negeri Para Bedebah is actually readable. It is easy for me to follow the story and to memorize even the side characters. The plot is superb, despite some of the lacks, such as the twist and some parts that need more detail. I love the simple story-telling, even though there are some technical terms that I don't understand (I don't want to stop the reading just because I want to look for the meaning of "kliring"). Still, this doesn't distract you to get the flow of the conflict. The part that I like the most is about the past story of Thomas as this brings a solid conflict throughout the story.<br /><br />Overall, for those who want to start reading a new genre of a novel (or even you are new to reading novel), I recommend you to add this novel to your cart.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3153606710079640000" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/924536173" />
    <a title="Tiara Amany (A Wave of Vellichor)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28837711-tiara-amany-a-wave-of-vellichor"><img alt="Tiara Amany (A Wave of Vellichor)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1469628888p2/28837711.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/924536173?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tiara Amany (A Wave of Vellichor)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tiara Amany (A Wave of Vellichor)" href="/user/show/28837711-tiara-amany-a-wave-of-vellichor">Tiara Amany (A Wave of Vellichor)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28837711-tiara-amany-a-wave-of-vellichor?shelf=indonesia">indonesia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28837711-tiara-amany-a-wave-of-vellichor?shelf=school-library">school-library</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28837711-tiara-amany-a-wave-of-vellichor?shelf=2012-published">2012-published</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28837711-tiara-amany-a-wave-of-vellichor?shelf=book-1">book-1</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28837711-tiara-amany-a-wave-of-vellichor?shelf=negeri-para-bedebah-series">negeri-para-bedebah-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/28837711-tiara-amany-a-wave-of-vellichor?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer924536173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18304695026585028254">Want me to describe it with just one word? Action.<br/><br/>This is my second Tere Liye read, the first one being a romance novel (Kau, Aku dan Sepucuk Angpau Merah). I've heard a lot of good things form Tere Liye, his book being made into movies and stuff, but I never had any interest in reading his books because his books' synopsis rarely reveal what the book is actually about, and I have a fear of reading books which can make you cry easily. And from what I heard, Tere Liye is good at those kind of boo</span>
  <span id="freeText18304695026585028254" style="display:none">Want me to describe it with just one word? Action.<br /><br />This is my second Tere Liye read, the first one being a romance novel (Kau, Aku dan Sepucuk Angpau Merah). I've heard a lot of good things form Tere Liye, his book being made into movies and stuff, but I never had any interest in reading his books because his books' synopsis rarely reveal what the book is actually about, and I have a fear of reading books which can make you cry easily. And from what I heard, Tere Liye is good at those kind of books (Hafalan Surat Delisa, etc.)<br /><br />It wasn't until high school that he does not only write tear-jerking novels, but also romance...and action ones.<br /><br />"Negeri Para Bedebah". Judging from the cover and the title, I previously thought that this book is about politics, and I hate politics. But a friend of mine said that his favorite author is Tere Liye, I thought that I ought to try to read more of his books. So I picked this one, the one that seemed the least tear-jerking one.<br /><br />It was a great read. <br /><br />There's this Thomas guy, a money consultant who has a dark past which estranged him from his uncle. And Maggie, the secretary, Julia, Kadek, and other characters. I was surprised at some points in the story because I didn't expect to turn out that way. But Thomas...he's a genius, a real fighter. I probably find him attractive and add him to my book-boyfriend list if not for his age, which is probably around 30s or 40s.<br /><br />Yeah, it does have some politics and stuff (we're talking about conspiracies and stuff here, people). Plus lots of economy words and terms, which I have no understanding of. But all in all, this is one good book.<br /><br />Just a trivia. I have a friend who is also a fellow book lover. He often asks me what am I currently reading. I once answered 'Bedebah', and I meant 'Negeri Para Bedebah', and he got paralyzed at first because he thought that I was cursing him. 'Bedebah' is a rude word to say in Indonesia. It's a curse or some sort, so it's impolite to say it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18304695026585028254" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NleqMnVbOtgCKTr4mUwz+kUzgL9Kql2dg20agjinr9N71tJ538OrTcOUHFqv+gYlyQpuOXU9ihwOfmNW6NGq3Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UyXPU8V1ppzKpYYLfaWLPdOowfksH5csVzfY2R0zaBgepLcYb+03CQsYoKlLE77iX5EvfxOIQK3aJKENzUVtFg==')})
  }

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/21394665-negeri-para-bedebah">Quotes from Negeri Para Bedebah</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Ketika satu kota dipenuhi orang miskin, kejahatan yang terjadi hanya level rendah, perampokan, mabuk-mabukan, atau tawuran. Kaum proletar seperti ini mudah diatasi, tidak sistematis dan jelas tidak memiliki visi misi, tinggal digertak, beres. Bayangkan ketika kota dipenuhi orang yang terlalu kaya, dan terus rakus menelan sumber daya di sekitarnya. Mereka sistematis, bisa membayar siapa saja untuk menjadi kepanjangan tangan, tidak takut dengan apapun. Sungguh tidak ada yang bisa menghentikan mereka selain sistem itu sendiri yang merusak mereka.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/740623-ketika-satu-kota-dipenuhi-orang-miskin-kejahatan-yang-terjadi-hanya">82 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;Dalam sebuah skenario infiltrasi ide jangan pernah peduli dengan latar belakang lawan biacara kalian. Konsep egaliter menemukan tempat sebenar-benarnya. Bahkan termasuk ketika kalian wawancara pekerjaan misalnya. Sekali kalian merasa sebagai "orang yang mencari pekerjaan" sementara mereka yang menyeleksi adalah "orang yang memegang leher masa depan kalian," tidak akan pernah ada dialog yang sejajar, pantas, dan mengesankan.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/1134733-dalam-sebuah-skenario-infiltrasi-ide-jangan-pernah-peduli-dengan-latar">21 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
